# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` containing a comprehensive analysis of the Firefox layout engine reflow architecture with:

### **Key Files Identified (94 total):**

1. **Frame Construction Pipeline**
   - `layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h` - Main frame construction logic
   - `layout/base/nsFrameManager.cpp/h` - Frame tree management

2. **Block Layout Reflow**
   - `layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h` - Core block layout algorithm
   - `layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h` - Reflow state management
   - `layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h` - Block reflow context
   - `layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h` - Inline line layout
   - `layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h` - Line box data structure

3. **Dirty Frame Invalidation**
   - `layout/generic/nsFrameState.cpp/h` - Frame state bits
   - `layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h` - State bit definitions
   - `layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h` - Style-based invalidation

4. **Supporting Systems**
   - Float management, Table layout, Flex/Grid layout
   - Pagination (printing), Ruby text, Multi-column layout
   - Core infrastructure (PresShell, nsPresContext, ReflowInput/Output)

The JSON file includes detailed documentation of the reflow pipeline's execution flow, from PresShell::DoReflow() entry point through frame construction, block layout, and dirty frame tracking mechanisms.

pipeline is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the gecko-dev repository. The pipeline consists of three main components:\\n\\n**1. Frame Construction (nsCSSFrameConstructor)**\\nFrame construction is managed by nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h located in layout/base/. This class is responsible for constructing the frame tree from the DOM tree based on CSS display properties. Key methods handle ContentAppended, ContentInserted, and frame reconstruction for style changes. The FrameConstructionItem and FrameConstructionData structures guide how frames should be created.\\n\\n**2. Block Layout Reflow Pipeline**\\nThe block layout reflow is the core of the layout engine:\\n\\n- **PresShell (layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h)**: The presentation shell is the main entry point for layout. It orchestrates the overall reflow process through methods like DoReflow() and manages dirty frames via FrameNeedsReflow().\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h)**: The primary block container frame implementation. The Reflow() method performs the actual block layout, handling floats, margins, and child frame positioning.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h)**: Maintains state during block reflow including float tracking, margin collapsing, and available space calculations.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h)**: Helper class for reflowing block frames, handling block-level child frames and their positioning.\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h)**: Manages inline content layout within lines. Handles span management, baseline calculations, and inline frame positioning. The ReflowFrame() method processes individual frames within a line.\\n\\n- **nsLineBox (layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h)**: Represents a line of inline content with cached metrics and dirty state. The line list (nsLineList) maintains all lines in a block.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput/ReflowOutput (layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h and ReflowOutput.cpp/h)**: Core data structures carrying reflow parameters (input constraints, spacing, etc.) and results (computed sizes, metrics, overflow areas).\\n\\n**3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism**\\nDirty frame tracking and invalidation is managed through several interconnected systems:\\n\\n- **Frame State Management (nsFrameState.cpp/h, nsFrameStateBits.h)**: Bit flags on frames track dirty states including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY, NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN, and NS_FRAME_NEEDS_REFLOW. These bits are checked and updated during reflow.\\n\\n- **nsIFrame Invalidation Methods (nsIFrame.cpp/h)**: Base frame class provides methods for invalidating frames and their subtrees. Methods like ChildIsDirty() in nsBlockFrame detect which children need reflow.\\n\\n- **Dirty Line Marking (nsBlockFrame.cpp)**: nsBlockFrame::LazyMarkLinesDirty() marks lines as dirty when needed. nsBlockFrame::ChildIsDirty() handles invalidation when child frames change.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h)**: Handles style invalidation that triggers reflow. ProcessAllPendingAttributeAndStateInvalidations() drives style-based dirty frame propagation.\\n\\n**Supporting Components**\\n\\nThe pipeline also includes specialized layout systems:\\n\\n- **Float Management (nsFloatManager.cpp/h)**: Tracks float positioning and available space around floats during line layout.\\n\\n- **Table Layout (layout/tables/)**: nsTableFrame, nsTableRowFrame, nsTableCellFrame, nsTableRowGroupFrame handle table-specific layout with specialized reflow logic.\\n\\n- **Flex/Grid Layout (nsFlexContainerFrame.cpp/h, nsGridContainerFrame.cpp/h)**: Modern layout algorithms using specialized reflow input/output.\\n\\n- **Inline Frame Handling (nsInlineFrame.cpp/h, nsFirstLetterFrame.cpp/h)**: Special inline container and pseudo-element handling.\\n\\n- **Printing Support (nsPageFrame, nsPageContentFrame, nsPageSequenceFrame)**: Paginated layout for print and preview modes.\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline executes through a top-down traversal starting from PresShell::DoReflow(), which initiates block reflow via nsBlockFrame::Reflow(). Each frame type implements the Reflow() virtual method accepting ReflowInput and returning ReflowOutput. Dirty frames are marked and processed incrementally, with RestyleManager triggering invalidations based on style changes detected through the Servo style system.\"\n}\n",

pipeline is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the gecko-dev repository. The pipeline consists of three main components:\\n\\n**1. Frame Construction (nsCSSFrameConstructor)**\\nFrame construction is managed by nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h located in layout/base/. This class is responsible for constructing the frame tree from the DOM tree based on CSS display properties. Key methods handle ContentAppended, ContentInserted, and frame reconstruction for style changes. The FrameConstructionItem and FrameConstructionData structures guide how frames should be created.\\n\\n**2. Block Layout Reflow Pipeline**\\nThe block layout reflow is the core of the layout engine:\\n\\n- **PresShell (layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h)**: The presentation shell is the main entry point for layout. It orchestrates the overall reflow process through methods like DoReflow() and manages dirty frames via FrameNeedsReflow().\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h)**: The primary block container frame implementation. The Reflow() method performs the actual block layout, handling floats, margins, and child frame positioning.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h)**: Maintains state during block reflow including float tracking, margin collapsing, and available space calculations.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h)**: Helper class for reflowing block frames, handling block-level child frames and their positioning.\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h)**: Manages inline content layout within lines. Handles span management, baseline calculations, and inline frame positioning. The ReflowFrame() method processes individual frames within a line.\\n\\n- **nsLineBox (layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h)**: Represents a line of inline content with cached metrics and dirty state. The line list (nsLineList) maintains all lines in a block.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput/ReflowOutput (layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h and ReflowOutput.cpp/h)**: Core data structures carrying reflow parameters (input constraints, spacing, etc.) and results (computed sizes, metrics, overflow areas).\\n\\n**3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism**\\nDirty frame tracking and invalidation is managed through several interconnected systems:\\n\\n- **Frame State Management (nsFrameState.cpp/h, nsFrameStateBits.h)**: Bit flags on frames track dirty states including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY, NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN, and NS_FRAME_NEEDS_REFLOW. These bits are checked and updated during reflow.\\n\\n- **nsIFrame Invalidation Methods (nsIFrame.cpp/h)**: Base frame class provides methods for invalidating frames and their subtrees. Methods like ChildIsDirty() in nsBlockFrame detect which children need reflow.\\n\\n- **Dirty Line Marking (nsBlockFrame.cpp)**: nsBlockFrame::LazyMarkLinesDirty() marks lines as dirty when needed. nsBlockFrame::ChildIsDirty() handles invalidation when child frames change.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h)**: Handles style invalidation that triggers reflow. ProcessAllPendingAttributeAndStateInvalidations() drives style-based dirty frame propagation.\\n\\n**Supporting Components**\\n\\nThe pipeline also includes specialized layout systems:\\n\\n- **Float Management (nsFloatManager.cpp/h)**: Tracks float positioning and available space around floats during line layout.\\n\\n- **Table Layout (layout/tables/)**: nsTableFrame, nsTableRowFrame, nsTableCellFrame, nsTableRowGroupFrame handle table-specific layout with specialized reflow logic.\\n\\n- **Flex/Grid Layout (nsFlexContainerFrame.cpp/h, nsGridContainerFrame.cpp/h)**: Modern layout algorithms using specialized reflow input/output.\\n\\n- **Inline Frame Handling (nsInlineFrame.cpp/h, nsFirstLetterFrame.cpp/h)**: Special inline container and pseudo-element handling.\\n\\n- **Printing Support (nsPageFrame, nsPageContentFrame, nsPageSequenceFrame)**: Paginated layout for print and preview modes.\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline executes through a top-down traversal starting from PresShell::DoReflow(), which initiates block reflow via nsBlockFrame::Reflow(). Each frame type implements the Reflow() virtual method accepting ReflowInput and returning ReflowOutput. Dirty frames are marked and processed incrementally, with RestyleManager triggering invalidations based on style changes detected through the Servo style system.\"\n}\n",
